GT Equivalence Verification (BPG11)
============================================================
GT: c0*(c1 - P/c2)*P + c3*P**c4 + c5*P*exp(-c6*t)
Candidate formulas: 54

GT (fixed) can be rewritten as a sum of four independent basis terms:
\[
\text{GT}(t,P)=A\,P \;+\; B\,P^2 \;+\; C\,P^{1/3} \;+\; D\,P\,e^{-kt}
\]
with fixed nonzero constants
- \(A=0.7124493718672418\)
- \(B=-0.7124493718672418/68.90600928530216\neq 0\)
- \(C=0.7124493718672418\neq 0\)
- \(D=0.7124493718672418\neq 0\)
- \(k=0.03459335742983884\neq 0\)

So any matching candidate must be able (by choosing its free constants) to produce **exactly**: a \(P^{1/3}\) term, a \(P^2\) term, a linear \(P\) term, and a \(P\exp(-kt)\) term, with **no extra** \(t\)-only terms, no extra \(P\)-powers, no logs/sin/max/etc, and the exponential must be in \(t\) only and multiplied by \(P\).

Now check candidates:

1. Has extra \( \sin(Pc6+c7)\) and constant \(c8\). To match GT for all \(P\), must set \(c5=0\) and \(c8=0\). Then can set \(c0=C\), \(c1=B\), \(c2+c3=A\), and choose \(c4=-k\), \(c3=D\). Works. **Match possible**.

2. Terms: \(P^2 c0\), \(P c1 (P c2)^{c3}= c1 c2^{c3} P^{1+c3}\), \(P c4 e^{c5 t}\), \(P c6\), constant \(c7\). To get \(P^{1/3}\) is impossible (only powers \(2\), \(1+c3\), and \(1\)). So **no**.

3. Has \(P^{c3} c4 e^{c5 t}\) and \(P^{c6}c7\) plus linear terms. To get \(P e^{-kt}\) requires \(c3=1\) and \(c5=-k\), but then still need separate \(P^{1/3}\) term: could set \(c6=1/3\). However then you also have *two* independent linear-in-\(P\) terms \(P c1 + P c2\) (fine, can combine), and \(P^2 c0\) (fine). But you also have the exponential term multiplied by \(P^{c3}\) (ok with \(c3=1\)). No extra constants if set \(c8=0\). This actually can reproduce all four GT components:
- set \(c0=B\)
- set \(c1+c2=A\)
- set \(c6=1/3,\; c7=C\)
- set \(c3=1,\; c4=D,\; c5=-k\)
- set \(c8=0\)
So **match possible**.

4. Similar to (2) but with two linear \(P\) terms and constant. Still lacks \(P^{1/3}\). **No**.

5. Has \(P^{1/3}\), \(P^2\), linear \(P\), and \(P e^{c4 t}\), plus \(P^{c5}c6\) and constant. To match GT, set \(c5=0\Rightarrow P^0 c6\) becomes constant; but GT has no constant, so must set \(c6=0\) and \(c7=0\). Then choose \(c0=C\), \(c1=B\), \(c2+c?=A\) (here linear is \(P c1 + P c2\) so set \(c1+c2=A\)), and set \(c3=D,\; c4=-k\). Works. **Match possible**.

6. Has \(P^{1/3}\), multiple \(P^2\) terms (can combine), multiple linear \(P\) terms (can combine), and \(P c6 e^{c7 t}\), plus constant \(c8\). Set \(c8=0\). Choose sums to match \(A,B\), set \(c0=C\), set \(c6=D,\; c7=-k\). Works. **Match possible**.

7. Has \(P^{1/3}\), \(P^2\) (two), linear \(P\) (two), and \(P c4 e^{c5 t}\), plus constant \(c7\). Set \(c7=0\). Combine coefficients to match \(A,B\), set \(c0=C\), set \(c4=D,\; c5=-k\). Works. **Match possible**.

8. Has \(P^{1/3}\), \(P^2\), linear \(P\) (two), and \(P c4 e^{c5 t}\), plus constant \(c6\). Set \(c6=0\). Combine linear coefficients to \(A\), set \(c1=B\), \(c0=C\), \(c4=D,\; c5=-k\). Works. **Match possible**.

9. Has \(P^{1/3}\), \(P^2\), linear \(P\), and \(P c3 e^{c4 t}\), plus constant \(c5\). Set \(c5=0\). Set \(c0=C\), \(c1=B\), \(c2=A\), \(c3=D\), \(c4=-k\). Works. **Match possible**.

10. Has \(P^2\), linear \(P\), \(P e^{c3 t}\), and \(P^{c4}c5\) plus constant. No \(P^{1/3}\) unless set \(c4=1/3\), but then you still need a *separate* \(P e^{-kt}\) term: you have \(P c2 e^{c3 t}\) (good). Then you can set constant \(c6=0\). This gives all four components:
- \(P^2 c0\) for \(B\)
- \(P c1\) for \(A\)
- \(P^{1/3} c5\) via \(c4=1/3\)
- \(P c2 e^{c3 t}\) for \(D e^{-kt}\) via \(c3=-k\)
So **match possible**.

11. Same as (9) but with extra \(c6 e^{c7 t}\max(0,-P+c8)\). To avoid non-GT piece for all \(P\), must set \(c6=0\). Also set \(c5=0\) to remove constant. Then reduces to (9) without constant and is matchable. **Match possible**.

12. Same as (9) but without constant: directly match by setting \(c0=C,c1=B,c2=A,c3=D,c4=-k\). **Match possible**.

13. Has extra \(c6\log(c7 e^{P^{c8}c9}+1)\) and constant \(c5\). Must set \(c6=0\) and \(c5=0\) to remove extras; then reduces to (9) without constant and is matchable. **Match possible**.

14. Has extra \(c5\log(Pc6+1)\) and constant \(c7\). Must set \(c5=0\) and \(c7=0\). Then reduces to (9) without constant and is matchable. **Match possible**.

15. Has rational terms \(P c5/(Pc6+c7)+c8/(Pc6+c7)\) and constant \(c9\). To remove them for all \(P\), easiest set \(c5=0,c8=0,c9=0\). Then match remaining as in (9). **Match possible**.

16. Has extra \(P c5\log(c6|P+c7|+1)\) and constant \(c8\). Must set \(c5=0\) and \(c8=0\). Then match remaining. **Match possible**.

17. Has \(P c2 (P c3)^{c4}=c2 c3^{c4} P^{1+c4}\) plus other linear terms and \(P e^{c7 t}\) and constant. To avoid unwanted power, set \(c2=0\) (or choose \(c4=0\) making it linear; either way can fold into linear). Set constant \(c9=0\). Then you still have \(P^{1/3}\), \(P^2\), linear \(P\) (several), and \(P e^{c7 t}\): matchable. **Match possible**.

18. Has \(P^3\) term which GT lacks; must set its coefficient \(c1=0\). Then has \(P^{1/3}\), multiple \(P^2\) terms, multiple linear \(P\) terms, and \(P e^{c8 t}\), plus constant \(c9\) (set to 0). Matchable. **Match possible**.

19. Has extra \(P^{c5}c6\) and constant. Set \(c6=0\) and \(c7=0\). Then reduces to (12). **Match possible**.

20. Has \(P^2\), linear \(P\), \(P^{c2}c3\), and \(P^{c4}c5 e^{c6 t}\), plus constant. Need \(P^{1/3}\) and \(P e^{-kt}\). Set \(c2=1/3, c3=C\). For exponential term, need power \(P^1\): set \(c4=1\), \(c5=D\), \(c6=-k\). Set constant \(c7=0\). Set \(c0=B\), \(c1=A\). Works. **Match possible**.

21. Extra sine-of-log term and constant \(c5\). Must set \(c6=0\) and \(c5=0\). Then reduces to (9) without constant and is matchable. **Match possible**.

Also constant \(c7\) must be 0. Then set \(c4=1/3,c5=C\); set \(c1=D,c2=-k\); set \(c0=B\); set \(c3=A\). Works. **Match possible**.

28. Has two power terms \(P^{c5}c6\) and \(P^{c7}c8\) plus constant. Can set one of them to \(P^{1/3}\) and kill the other by coefficient 0; set constant 0. Then match remaining as (9). **Match possible**.

29. Has \(P*P^{c1}c2 = c2 P^{1+c1}\) plus linear terms and \(P^{c5}c6 e^{c7 t}\). Need \(P^{1/3}\) and \(P e^{-kt}\). Exponential term can be \(P e^{-kt}\) by setting \(c5=1, c6=D, c7=-k\). For \(P^{1/3}\), need \(1+c1=1/3\Rightarrow c1=-2/3\) and set \(c2=C\). Then set \(c0=B\) and combine linear \(P c3 + P c4\) to \(A\). Set constant \(c8=0\). Works. **Match possible**.

30. Has extra \(c8/t^{1/5}\) and constant \(c9\). Must set \(c8=0,c9=0\). Remaining still lacks \(P^{1/3}\) (only \(P^2\), \(P^{1+c3}\), and \(P\)). So **no**.

31. Same issue as (30): must set \(c7=0,c8=0\) but still no \(P^{1/3}\). **No**.

32. Has extra rational-in-\(t\) terms \(P c5/(c6 t+c7)+c8/(c6 t+c7)\) and constant \(c9\). To match GT (no such terms), set \(c5=0,c8=0,c9=0\). Then reduces to (12) and matches. **Match possible**.

35. Has \(P c3/(c4+t)^2\) (non-exponential \(t\)-dependence) and \(P c5 e^{c6 t}\). GT has only \(P e^{-kt}\) as \(t\)-dependence. Must set \(c3=0\) to remove rational term. Then can set \(c5=D,c6=-k\). Constant \(c7=0\). Then match remaining \(P^{1/3},P^2,P\). **Match possible**.
